patch 8.1.0768: updating completions may cause the popup menu to flicker ¬∑ vim/vim@ae65438
Problem: Updating completions may cause the popup menu to flicker. Solution: Avoid updating the text below the popup menu before drawing the popup menu.

func Test_listchars_halfwidth()
  enew!
  set ff=unix
  set list

  set listchars+=space:_
  call append(0, [
          \ ' „Çõ    „Çú'
          \ ])
  let expected = [
          \ '_„Çõ^I„Çú$',
          \ ]
  redraw!
  call cursor(1, 1)
  let got = ScreenLines(1, virtcol('$'))
  bw!
  set listchars& ff&
  call assert_equal([expected], got)
endfunction
